Page 11

Kidnapping Case of Lin Weiqing Two Years Ago

Key Suspect Chen Baofu Arrested

Chen Baofu Was a Concession Police Officer

Motivated to Kidnap Due to Unpaid Rent to Lin

Lin Weiqing, brother of Lin Biao, president of the Suzhou High Court, was an architect residing at 55 Baikai'er Road. On the evening of February 8, 1931, Lin, accompanied by his wife and sister, returned home in his car, license number 3733. Upon arriving at the entrance, they were suddenly confronted by several kidnappers who brandished pistols and threatened to kidnap them. Seeing the situation was bad, Lin resisted and engaged in a struggle with the kidnappers. As a result, Lin and his sister escaped, but his wife was unable to escape and was held in the car under the kidnappers' watch. They sped away, and when they arrived at the intersection of Minhang Road and Broadway Road in Hongkou, the car suddenly stopped due to a mechanical issue. Seeing an opportunity, Lin's wife lied to the kidnappers, claiming that the car had run out of gasoline. The kidnappers panicked and believing her, fled the scene. Afterwards, Lin's wife reported the incident to the Huishan police station, which sent detectives to investigate. Lin's bodyguard, Wang Jiakui, was suspected to be involved in the case. Under normal circumstances, when Lin returned home by car, he would honk the horn, and Wang would open the door upon hearing the sound. However, on that day, Wang did not immediately open the door, and when he finally did, he immediately closed it after seeing the kidnappers, preventing Lin's wife from escaping. The police arrested Wang Jiakui, who confessed to having conspired with a man named Chen Baofu to kidnap Lin Weiqing. Chen Baofu was the main instigator and operated the Longquan Tea House on Qiwupu Road. The detectives took Wang to arrest Chen, but Chen had already fled. Only a photo of Chen was found. Wang was sent to the First Special District Court, which sentenced him to death in the first instance. However, the provincial government sent the case back for retrial, and Wang's sentence was reduced to 12 years in prison. Chen Baofu remained at large for two years. Until recently, detectives from the Jing'an Temple police station arrested Chen and sent him to the First Special District Court for interrogation. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Tingqi continued the trial in the eighth criminal court. Police lawyer Li Zhishan stated the facts, saying that Chen was being prosecuted under Article 1, Paragraph [blank] of the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits. The defendant had confessed to the police that the house of the Longquan Tea House he ran belonged to Lin Weiqing, and because he was in arrears with the rent for several months, Lin wanted to sue him. Chen then colluded with Lin's bodyguard Wang Jiakui and the fugitive Wang Yaoxi to carry out the kidnapping. A written confession was presented for review, and it was requested that a thorough investigation be conducted. The defendant Chen Baofu testified that he had been a doorman at the Public Works Department for many years and was acquainted with Wang Jiakui. He had an argument with Wang over rent collection, which led to a fight. However, he had no prior knowledge of the kidnapping case and was falsely accused by Wang. Wang Jiakui was also brought from the Western Prison for questioning by Judge Wu. His answers were evasive and he was unwilling to speak clearly. The court ruled that the case required further investigation and ordered Chen Baofu to be returned to custody for further questioning.

A Comedy

Married for Eight Days, Sleeping Separately

Groom Suspicious, Bride Wrongfully Accused

Coroner's Examination Reveals the Truth

Wang A'da, a 23-year-old farmer from Wangjiapaolou, twelve miles north of Wusong, married Miss Chen (17 years old), the daughter of Mrs. Chen Yang, a rural woman from Wusong Town, on April 13th of this year. However, after the marriage, both the bride and groom were young and unsophisticated, and they were often shy, so they did not talk for several days. At night, they slept on the same bed but had different dreams, with quilts separating them, and no intimate relations occurred. After eight days, the bride returned to her mother's home in Ningbo. She was going to stay at her mother's, but then the red tide [menstruation] came, and she was superstitious so she stayed at her mother's. However, Wang A'da felt neglected because his bride had been cold to him for eight days after the marriage, and now she had gone home and not returned. Moreover, his mother-in-law had remarried Wang Beiyao, who ran a pancake shop. In the past, the mother and daughter had lived in the same room as the stepfather, and he suspected that his wife had an affair with her stepfather. Therefore, suspicions arose, and he rushed to his wife's home the day before yesterday. He saw that his wife's family only had one room, and he concluded that his stepfather-in-law was having an affair with his wife. He reported to the First Branch of the Seventh District, and Wang Zhaoyao, Chen Yang, and Wang Chen were arrested and sent to the local court for questioning yesterday. When Prosecutor Xie Lian opened the court for questioning, Wang A'da claimed that after his wife married him, he slept inside the quilt and she slept on top of the quilt, and she did not call him. Now that she has returned to Ningbo, she has not returned. When he went to call her, she was sleeping with her stepfather. Wang Chen claimed, "I am a bride. Only the groom calls the bride. There is no reason for a bride to be ashamed. As for the false accusation that I am having an affair with my stepfather, I ask for an examination. But I will not give up if my reputation is damaged." Wang Zhaoyao testified, "I am 40 years old, and I am also a child from a family of poetry and rites. My father was once a magistrate in Guangdong. I am poor now, but I do not do shameless things. If my reputation is damaged, I ask for retaliation." Chen Yang testified, "Although I have remarried, I have always supervised my daughter well. An examination can be conducted." After much debate between the two sides, the judge ordered a medical examination and found that the bride was a virgin. As a result, the truth was revealed, and the bride's side was outraged, demanding compensation for her reputation. The judge repeatedly persuaded them for a long time and ordered the two sides to go outside to negotiate a settlement.

Barbering and Other Industries

Please Negotiate the Gao Case

Decision to Request Negotiation According to Law to Value Life

Since the occurrence of the murder of barber Gao Yatouzi by French police officer No. 39, Milihong, on Albert Road, Nanchianjiatang in the French Concession, barbering colleagues throughout the city, and fellow Yangzhou natives in Shanghai, have been deeply angered by the French police officer's disregard for Chinese lives. Yesterday morning and afternoon, barbering colleagues and the Yangzhou Fellow Countrymen's Association convened special member meetings to discuss negotiation methods. The details are as follows:

All-Barbering Colleague Assembly

The Shanghai Barbering Guild, Pushan Hall, after receiving a report that Gao Yatouzi, an apprentice at the Hushunyuan Barber Shop, was innocently kicked to death by French police officer No. 39, Milihong, of the Shanzhong Road police station in the French Concession, on the morning of May 7th, barbers throughout the city were deeply indignant and demanded that a city-wide barbering colleague assembly be convened to discuss countermeasures. The guild convened a special member meeting around 10:00 AM yesterday, attended by over 300 barbering colleagues from the north and south cities and the British and French concessions. Zhou Lianze, a representative from the city party headquarters, attended to provide guidance. Chen Sijiang, Su Guangdian, and Zhang Yujin were publicly elected as the presidium. After performing the ritual, they silently mourned the deceased for three minutes. (1) Chairman Chen Sijiang reported on the purpose of the meeting, stating that the details of Gao Yatouzi's death have been seen in previous reports, but the French coroner's examination claimed that there were no injuries and that the death was due to illness. During the coroner's examination, only the upper body of the corpse was examined, and the injured part of the lower body was not examined. If it was said that he was ill, a 15-year-old child could still carry burdens and do business, so there are doubts about the court's coroner's examination. However, there are many witnesses who witnessed Gao Yatouzi being driven to death at the time, and it will not be difficult to prove it in detail in the future. But today's meeting is very enthusiastic, which shows that when there is injustice, people speak out, and everyone has the same heart. This matter concerns international lives, so how should we deal with it? Please discuss it. (2) Zhou Lianze, a representative from the city party headquarters, gave a speech saying that today, he represents the city party headquarters and attends, not because of his relationship with the colleagues, but because the tragic case of Gao Yatouzi concerns law, diplomacy, and lives. In his opinion, your guild should be reorganized into a colleague association according to law, so that you can get legal protection. However, the reorganization procedures cannot be completed in a short time. Now, regarding the tragic case, it is especially urgent to handle it. On the one hand, please ask Lawyer Wu Kaisheng to proceed according to law, and on the other hand, submit a request to various agencies to negotiate with the French authorities, so as to achieve the desired goal. (3) Gao Yuanlin, the father of the deceased, and Guo Wanhai, the representative of the shop owner, Hushunyuan, successively reported on the incident and the situation of the corpse's family. (4) Representatives from all walks of life expressed their opinions, generally paying attention to the goals and negotiation policies. (5) Resolution to demand goals: (A) Punish the murderer severely and execute him on the spot. (B) Provide generous compensation to the family of the deceased and maintain the aftermath. (C) Compensate for the loss of life to value personality. (D) Express an apology to our officials and people. (E) Guarantee that it will not happen again in the future (must be done in writing). (F) Improve policing and maintain public safety. (G) Add senior Chinese officials to the police station. (H) Use more Chinese police and fewer Western police. (I) Chinese directors and commissioners must have real power. (J) Request a review to clarify the truth. The above methods were all passed. (6) Discussion of the policy of coping with negotiations: (A) Submit requests to the competent authorities to negotiate with the French authorities. (B) Send a letter to the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the French Concession to assist in the negotiations. (C) When necessary, elect representatives to make a large petition to various agencies and groups. (D) Hire Lawyer Wu Kaisheng as a legal advisor to handle the case according to law on behalf of the family. (E) Organize a support association for the tragic case to handle all procedures. (F) Send a letter to various newspapers to do their best to publicize, and the entire colleague industry is responsible. (G) Improve the organization of this industry and discuss it separately. (H) Elect 19 executive committee members to be responsible for the execution of the resolution. (The names of the people are omitted. After the above methods were discussed and passed, hundreds of yuan were immediately recognized as negotiation expenses, and the five standing committee members, Luo Chuntao, Wei Tongyi, Chen Siqiao, Zhang Yujin, and Qian Shousen, were responsible for the safekeeping and payment until about 2:00 PM, when the meeting was adjourned. The atmosphere at the meeting was extremely tense, and it was an unprecedented gathering in the Shanghai barbering industry.

Yangzhou Fellow Countrymen's Joint Meeting Regarding the Gao Yatouzi case, the Yangzhou Fellow Countrymen's Association in Shanghai, in addition to sending letters to the Shanghai Municipal Party Committee, the French Consul's Office, the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the French Concession, the Citizens' Federation, the Business Federation, the French Chief Inspector, the Second Special District Court, the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Municipal Social Bureau, and other agencies and groups, asking them to severely punish the murderer, appease the family of the deceased, and ensure that it will not happen again in the future, and to negotiate immediately, also convened a special joint meeting of members yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. Dozens of people were present in the hall. Gao Yuanlin, the father of the deceased, and representatives of various groups were also present. Shen Dingchen, a standing committee member of the association, presided over the meeting, reporting on the purpose of the meeting and the process, which were roughly the same. Then, Lawyer Qian Shusheng stood up and expressed his legal opinions and the significance of various groups assisting in the negotiations. Next, Tang Huaxuan, a representative of the Barbering Guild, reported on the results of the industry's meeting and explained in detail the required goals and coping methods discussed. Next, Tong Lizhang, a representative of the French Concession group, proposed that a joint committee should be organized to collect opinions from all parties, summarize and submit them together, so as to avoid differences of opinion and instead be more unfavorable. Then, Gao Yuanlin, the father of the deceased, and Guo Wanhai, the representative of the shop owner, also attended and reported on everything, which was the same. (Omitted. Finally, it was resolved that the following should be handled first: (1) Publicly hire lawyers Qian Shusheng, E Sen, and Song Shixiang to join forces with Lawyer Wu Kaisheng to handle the negotiations. (2) Request the court to review the corpse and ask to temporarily keep the corpse for review. Chinese doctors should also be requested to participate in the review. (3) The negotiation policy and required goals should be consistent with the barbering industry. (4) The members of the association participating in the tragic case committee will be re-elected at a meeting tomorrow. (5) The committee of various groups jointly assisting the Gao Yatou case will be convened by the Yangzhou Fellow Countrymen's Association, and a meeting will be scheduled separately. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

British American Tobacco Company Reduces Work Hours

Workers Cross the River to Petition

Minor Conflict Occurs During the Rush

The Union Is Trying to Resolve the Issue

Due to the influence of the current situation, the British American Tobacco Company has experienced sluggish sales of all its products and a gradual increase in inventory. Therefore, the board of directors has decided to gradually reduce work hours at the First Factory in Lujiazui, Pudong, the Second Factory in Lujiazhai, and the Third Factory in Hudong. The work hours have been reduced from six days a week to five days, and then to four days since last month. There are tens of thousands of male and female workers in the three factories. Initially, it was assumed that the reduction in work hours was entirely due to the company's poor business performance, and that the reduction of one or two days per week was unavoidable and would not significantly affect livelihoods, so it was not appropriate to oppose it immediately. However, starting this week, the company has announced to the workers of the three factories that they will continue to reduce work hours by one day, and in reality, they will only work three days a week and rest four days. The average monthly salary has been reduced by half. At a time when prices are high, it is really difficult to maintain a living. It is even more difficult for those who have a family of several people relying on one person to work to barely make a living. As a result, it has aroused strong opposition from the workers. Yesterday, the Third Factory took the lead in launching the protest, gathering hundreds of people, and crossing the river to Pudong by boat, rushing into the First and Second Factories, instructing the workers not to accept the factory's announcement of halving work hours. When rushing in, the guards at the door tried to stop them because of the large number of people, causing a minor conflict, but it quickly calmed down, so the order was still good. It is now reported that the workers believe that the factory's continued reduction in work hours will really make it difficult to maintain their livelihoods, so they are demanding that the union negotiate with the company. After receiving the report, the Fifth District Cigarette Industry Union believed that the factory had previously guaranteed at least 35 hours of work per week, but now suddenly continued to reduce work hours, which was really wrong. In addition to immediately sending a letter to the factory to lodge a serious protest, it also convened an emergency joint meeting of the executive supervisors at 6:00 PM that night to discuss countermeasures. At the same time, the workers of the Huxi Taopeng Road branch also responded yesterday and announced a strike, expressing the same opposition as the Pudong branches.

Assassination of Feng Deqian

Li Minghui Testified in Court Yesterday

Wang Nengxiang Still Asks the Court to Investigate the Evidence

Li Minghui Failed to Identify the Face of the Murderer

Movie star Li Minghui fell in love with wealthy businessman Zheng Guoyou in Hong Kong last spring, but then abandoned Zheng and fell in love with Feng Deqian. Zheng became jealous, wanting to put Feng to death for taking his beloved. He instructed his chauffeur Liu Xing to find a way to kill Feng for 2,000 Hong Kong dollars to vent his anger. Liu then entrusted Xu Yongchen and Wang Nengxiang with the task. On March 24th at 8:30 PM, when Feng and Li were walking hand in hand on the Star Ferry Pier (road name), they used a pistol to kill Feng. Wang Nengxiang fled to Shanghai after the incident. Lu Liankui, the chief Chinese detective of the Public Concession Police, arrested Wang and sent him to the First Special District Court. Wang was found guilty and sentenced to life imprisonment. Wang refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court. The case has been heard once, but because the subpoenaed witness Li Minghui did not arrive, and it was also necessary to investigate in Guangzhou, the hearing was postponed. Yesterday afternoon was the date for the continued hearing. The Western detective in charge of the case accompanied witness Li Minghui to the First Criminal Court of the Second Branch of the High Court at 1:50 PM. At 2:00 PM, Yu Hua, the head of the Criminal Court of the Second Branch of the High Court, Zhao and Jiang, the two judges, and Prosecutor Zhong took their seats. Police lawyer Gan Jingxian and Wang Nengxiang's lawyer Zhao Chuanding were also present in court. Judge Yu first announced that the appellant requested that evidence be investigated at the Dadong Gramophone Company on Taiping North Road in Guangzhou. The court had entrusted the Guangzhou Local Court to conduct the investigation. Now, according to the reply, there is no Dadong Gramophone Company, so it is impossible to investigate. Wang Nengxiang then claimed that the main store of the Dadong Company is located at 52-54 Wangjiao Road in Hong Kong, and a branch was opened in Guangzhou on Taiping North Road in 1919, located on the east side of the Taiping Theater, which can be investigated. The court then summoned Li Minghui to the court. According to her testimony, on the night in question, when she and Feng Delian were walking hand in hand, she saw a man following behind them, only four or five steps away. She told Feng, but Feng did not pay attention. About two minutes later, she heard a loud sound, and Feng said that he had been hit. But because it was dark at the time, she could

Summer

Military Training Changes Methods

Liu Zhan'en Arrived in Nanjing Yesterday to Explain Difficulties

(Nanjing, 10th Dispatch) The Ministry of Education previously issued an order to all secondary and higher schools nationwide to uniformly implement strict military training for three weeks during the summer vacation. All universities cited various difficulties due to economic conditions and equipment, making it difficult to implement immediately. They specially sent a representative, Liu Zhan'en, to Nanjing to request the Ministry of Education and the Directorate-General of Training to postpone implementation temporarily. Liu Zhan'en arrived in Nanjing on the morning of the 10th and immediately visited Minister Wang, Vice Minister Duan, Director Shen of the Higher Education Department of the Ministry of Education, and Deputy Director Zhou of the Directorate-General of Training to explain various implementation difficulties. The Ministry of Education and the Directorate-General of Training will confer on modified methods. This year, it is planned to request local military authorities to accept students from various schools to train directly in the military for three weeks. Detailed methods will be announced jointly by the two departments soon.

The Ministry of Education Provides Relief to Northeastern Students

The Ministry of Education, concerned that government-funded students from the four provinces in the Northeast who are studying abroad are experiencing financial difficulties due to the loss of territory, sent a special letter to our embassies abroad on the 9th to investigate the situations of students from the Eastern Provinces separately to find ways to provide relief.

August 1st to 7th

Various Colleges Recruit First-Year Students and Third-Year Transfer Students

(Nanjing, 10th Dispatch) The Enrollment Committee of National Central University held a meeting on the 10th and decided to enroll 350 first-year students in the Colleges of Arts, Sciences, Law, Education, Engineering, Agriculture, and Commerce this afternoon. Various departments can recruit third-year transfer students. Examinations will be held in four locations: the university's campuses in Nanjing, Beiping, Wuchang, and Guangzhou. The registration period is from July 21st to 27th, and the examination period is from August 1st to 7th.

Boy Scouts

Regulations for Filing Training Courses for Instructors

The Ministry of Education issued an order to the Departments and Bureaus of Education in various provinces and cities, stating: "It is approved by the Headquarters of the Boy Scouts of China that 'the regulations and curricula of the Boy Scout instructor training courses organized in various places are not uniform. They neither submit applications to higher-level authorities for guidance and supervision in advance, nor do they submit reports of the process for filing afterward. Such arbitrary actions are detrimental to the spirit of the Boy Scouts. The Headquarters has formulated the Regulations for Filing Training Courses for Boy Scout Instructors of China and submitted them to the fourth meeting of the Preparatory Committee for approval. In addition to issuing separate letters to the Party Headquarters and Boy Scout Councils in various provinces and cities for information, a copy of the regulations is enclosed and sent to your Ministry for review. In the future, if secondary schools and specialized physical education schools in various places establish Boy Scout instructor training courses, they must follow these regulations. It is hoped that you will instruct your subordinates to take note.'" A copy of the Regulations for Filing Training Courses for Boy Scout Instructors of China is enclosed. The original document is being sent with this order so that your subordinates in secondary schools and specialized physical education schools can take note. This order. Regulations for Filing Training Courses for Boy Scout Instructors of China

(1) All secondary schools, specialized physical education schools, and Party Headquarters in various parts of the country that establish Boy Scout instructor training courses must file with the Headquarters of the Boy Scouts of China in accordance with these regulations. (2) Those requesting to file must submit detailed reports of the training course's regulations, funding sources, training dates, and number of trainees to the Headquarters of the Boy Scouts of China for approval. (3) All training curricula must follow the curriculum standards prescribed by the Boy Scouts of China. (4) After the training course begins, the Headquarters may send personnel to inspect or designate a member of the local council to be responsible for the investigation and reporting. (5) If, after inspection, the training course is deemed to have areas for improvement, the Headquarters may order corrections at any time. (6) When the training course is completed and graduation examinations are held, a request must be submitted to the Headquarters to send personnel to supervise the examination. (7) Graduation certificates for training personnel who pass the graduation examination supervised and verified by personnel sent by the Headquarters may be stamped with the Headquarters' seal. (8) The style of the graduation certificate for the training course must comply with the regulations of the Headquarters (the certificate style will be determined separately). (9) If there are any matters not covered by these regulations, they will be amended by the Headquarters of the Boy Scouts of China. (10) These regulations shall be promulgated and implemented by the Headquarters of the Boy Scouts of China.

Yu Dawei Donates Memorial Scholarship for Deceased Friend

Applicants Limited to National Central University Students

(Nanjing, 10th Dispatch) Yu Dawei, Director of the Ordnance Department and Professor at National Central University, donated the remuneration given to him by National Central University as a memorial scholarship for his deceased friend, the former National Central University Professor Jin Jingyang. Various Cultural Organizations

Initiate an Academic National Salvation Movement Week

Decide to Organize a Joint Office for Various Cultural Organizations

Designate May Fourth as the Commemoration Day for the Cultural Renaissance Movement

And Raise Funds to Establish an Educational Bank and an Academic Club

The Shanghai Cultural Organizations' May Fourth Commemoration Meeting was held yesterday at 1 PM at the University Educational Association in the Continental Arcade. The meeting adjourned.

Student Speech and Essay Contests at Various Universities to be Held

Preparatory Meeting Held Yesterday

Various Schools to Begin Preliminary Rounds Immediately

The preparatory meeting for the speech, debate, and essay contests for students of various universities in Shanghai was held yesterday at 4 PM at the University Educational Association. Zhang Shouyong from Guanghua University, Zheng Hongnian (represented by Yang Yufen) from Jinan University, Kang Xuanyi from the University Educational Association, Lei Guoneng from Daxia University, Huang Xianzhang from Jiangnan University, Chen Jilie from the College of Law and Political Science, Cheng Ruikun from the College of Culture, and more than 20 principals and deans of students from various universities attended. Kang Xuanyi chaired the meeting. (甲) Reporting Matters: Zhang Shouyong and others reported that the preliminary round dates for Guanghua University are before the 19th of this month, Jinan University before the 20th, Jiangnan University before the 20th, and Culture and Law and Political Science and Daxia Universities are all in the process of holding them. (乙) Matters Decided: (1) Deciding on the topics: It was decided that (甲) the English debate topic would be: "Assuming that Chinese universities in the future should only offer four disciplines: agriculture, engineering, medicine, and science." The Chinese debate topic would be: "China should immediately establish an educational bank." (乙) The Chinese essay topic would be: "A concrete plan for academic national salvation." The English essay topic would be: "A concrete plan for an educational bank." (丙) The speech topic would be freely chosen. (2) The method of producing representatives: It was decided that preliminary rounds would be held independently by each school, and each school would produce one representative for Chinese and English speeches, and one team each for the affirmative and negative sides of the debate, with three people per team, and one person per school for essays, all within this month. (3) The case of stipulating speech time: It was decided that each person would be limited to eight minutes. (4) Recommendation of Mr. Xi Yushu to solicit prizes from the banking community. (5) How to nominate judges: It was decided that each school would hire its own judges for the preliminary rounds, and the finals should invite a third party unrelated to the two schools involved. (6) Date and location of the speech finals: It was decided to be tentatively set for June 3rd at a location in the central area of the city. (7) A copy of this resolution will be sent to the University Student Union for cooperation.

Female Students from Provincial High Schools Arrive in Shanghai for Observation

A group of twelve people from the graduating class of the Anhui Provincial Fifth Women's High School's senior high school and normal departments' educational observation group, led by the school's education instructor Mr. Zhang Zhenyong, arrived in Shanghai for observation and arrived in port a few days ago. They have been visiting elementary schools such as Wan Zhu and Xi Cheng in the Eastern District, as well as public education centers. On the 9th, they visited Daxia University, where Professors Dong Renjian and Huang Jingsi gave lectures. Yesterday, they visited elementary schools in the Western District and took a train to Hangzhou in the evening. It is reported that they will stay in Hangzhou for five days and then return to Yingzhou via Wuxian.

International Education Society

Yesterday, Mr. Cheng Qibao Gave a Lecture

The Shanghai International Education Society held a general meeting of its members at the YMCA in the Eight Immortals Bridge area the other day. They specially invited Mr. Cheng Qibao, a specialist sent by the Ministry of Education to Europe to study education, to give a lecture. More than a hundred Chinese and foreign members attended. Dr. Li Zhaohuan, the president, was unable to attend due to business and was represented by Mr. Lanhua Da. The meeting began with an introductory speech by committee member Chen Heqin, followed by a lecture by Professor Cheng Qibao. Mr. Cheng first described the characteristics of the educational systems of Britain, the United States, France, Germany, Italy, Russia, and Poland, the trends in future facilities, and his personal observations. He then mentioned the promotion of civic education, asserting that an excellent environment must be created from the natural aspect and that the government and the education sector must fully cooperate. His reasoning was thorough and moved the audience. Finally, Mr. Cheng briefly mentioned the emphasis on students' political training in Italy and Russia, but did not make any affirmative judgment. The meeting adjourned around 8 o'clock.

Graduates of Xinlu Normal School Visit

Twenty-seven students from the senior high school normal department's third-year class and thirty-eight students from the rural normal department's third-year class of the Shanghai Municipal Xinlu Normal School will all graduate this semester. The senior normal third-year graduation examinations and the first round of trial teaching have all been completed. Therefore, from the 9th of this month, they will be led by the school's internship instructor to visit various elementary schools in Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Suzhou, and other places for two weeks to learn from each other. As the rural normal third-year class's first round of trial teaching has not yet been completed, it is scheduled to visit Beijing from May 16th. It is reported that after the graduating class students return to school from their visits, they will hold a second round of trial teaching. In addition to the affiliated Jiazi Elementary School, which the school already has, the Municipal Education Bureau has also designated the municipal Wan Zhu, Xi Cheng, Yang Zheng, Shi Hua, Gao Chang, Yong Ning, and Du Chuan seven elementary schools to conduct trial teaching for four weeks to emphasize practice.

Fudan University to Hold Summer School

Fudan University, in order to increase opportunities for young people to study, will use the summer vacation to establish a summer school, from July 10th to August 10th. Registration will be around the beginning of July. All students studying at universities at home and abroad and high school graduates may register for the summer school. Jiangnan University Volleyball Champion Fudan Team (Photo by Wang Kai)

Difficult to Distinguish

Fudan won the first set, Daxia took back the second, Fudan won the third set, and Daxia won the fourth set, making it a tense situation that could not be resolved. In these four sets, there were several bitter battles before the winner was decided. In the first set, when Daxia was leading with 19 to 17, Fudan chased 14 points to win the first set. The situation was similar in the second set. Fudan had the advantage in the third set, and Daxia fought bravely to win back the fourth set, making it an even situation of two to two.

Complete Collapse

After being one to two down, Daxia worked hard in the fourth set, with success or failure hanging in the balance, and won the fourth set. After this fierce battle, they passed safely through the storm. In the fifth set, they suddenly showed an inability to stabilize and were so flustered that they could not recover. Fudan's attacks were completely unopposed. Daxia only scored one point. Fudan ended the set with two players serving, and the world was suddenly decided, which was unexpected.

Introductory Remarks: The True Meaning of Fashion

— Yang An

When clothing is called "fashion," most people automatically think of it as being trendy or modern. But what does "modern" really mean? What are the standards for being modern? What does "trendy" mean, and what are its boundaries? Try asking someone if they can answer these questions. Without standards or boundaries, it's not worthy of being called "fashion." In my opinion, the meaning of "fashion" has three aspects:

First, it's about aesthetics. Loving beauty is human nature. Not just adults, but even small children like to wear beautiful clothes. Look at a child in the family. If you put a nice new outfit on them today, they'll be excited and proud, with an indescribable expression. Generally, the standards for beauty are: first, elegance; second, cleanliness; and third, simplicity. What is most taboo is vulgarity, rudeness, or strangeness.

Second, the true meaning of fashion is suitability. Mr. Hu Shi said, "There's no such thing as fashionable or unfashionable, only suitable or unsuitable. What is suitable is fashionable, and what is unsuitable is unfashionable." For example, in today's busy world, agility is valued. If we were to still wear the wide robes and large sleeves of centuries past, it would not only be unsuitable but would also make us a laughingstock. Therefore, suitable clothing should have the following three standards: first, convenience; second, economy; and third, simplicity. What is most taboo is being cumbersome, extravagant, or complicated.

Third, the essence of fashionable clothing is hygiene. Fashion must be hygienic. Narrow sleeves hinder movement, and constricted chests impede development. Furthermore, heavy fur and thick cotton easily lead to a decreased ability to withstand the cold. None of these can be considered fashionable. Hygienic fashion should first be in accordance with the seasons, second be in line with science, and third be moderate. What is most taboo is disregarding the climate, going against science, or being excessive or insufficient.

Taking advantage of the China National Goods Company holding a national goods fashion convention, this publication has created this special issue on fashion to encourage the Chinese people to pay attention to fashion and to correct the common misunderstanding of the true meaning of fashion. Therefore, we present these three main points as a contribution to those in society who are interested in Chinese-made fashion.

Old Women's National Goods Fashion

— Rui Shousong

If we go to the streets or crowded markets, especially during grand temple festivals, we can easily see that most "old and decrepit" old women who walk with a sway wear national goods—shirts made of Shilin silk and trousers made of white homespun cloth. On their feet are pointed shoes made of black twill or black satin. Some old women even embroider beautiful wildflowers or even the characters "Longevity and Wealth," and "Blessings and Longevity." Some old women also wear osmanthus flowers and wild roses in their hair. To fashionable people, this decoration must be scorned as "outdated" and "pedantic," but in the minds of the old women, it is indeed the epitome of fashion!

It's not that they don't have money to use "foreign devils' national goods," but they can't manage them. It's not that they don't have the ability to "loudly advocate for national goods," but they feel that loudly advocating is embarrassing and not very effective. Only by burying themselves in the work can they be effective!

Furthermore, they admit that their prime has passed. In the course of their lives, they have shed countless drops of sweat and used countless amounts of energy. Now that they are old, they can finally enjoy a peaceful life. Therefore, wearing that kind of national goods fashion is both a way to express "enjoying their twilight years" and a way to commemorate the hard work and sweat they have shed in the past!

Baby's Cries

— Qian

It was a rainy morning, probably around the Qingming Festival? Gusts of northeast wind still brought some chill. The eldest daughter of the second landlord was preparing her schoolbag as usual, getting ready to go to school. Perhaps it was her mother's love that made her want her to wear more clothes. "Mom! Don't need to wear more! It looks ugly; with this scarf, I don't feel cold." I heard the eldest daughter say this, and it caught my attention. I thought, could the warmth of a scarf warm the whole body? Because time was tight, I couldn't bother with idle chatter and left with my umbrella.

As someone who sits at a desk all day, I didn't get home to rest until after 5:00 PM. As soon as I stepped into the doorway, Wang's six-year-old daughter! Baby, was crying like a slaughtered pig. I always hate being bothered, so I walked over to take a look. I saw Baby desperately pulling at the eldest daughter's scarf. Mrs. Wang, however, scolded angrily: "It will fade soon enough. What is it good for! When you grow up, I will ask your father to spend five dollars to buy you a foreign one."

At this time, I became impatient and said, "Mrs. Wang, why don't you make her one! Anyway, it's easy to do with two or three dimes. Although this lined flannel isn't as good as foreign serge, it's still beautiful and doesn't fade. Many families, big and small, buy it to make qipaos and scarves! As for the five-dollar foreign scarves, I advise you not to buy them! If there are good national goods to replace them, why buy foreign goods, especially when the Japanese are invading!" Mrs. Wang was, of course, not satisfied with my philosophical speech, but she couldn't resist Baby's crying, so she took advantage of the free time, dragged the eldest daughter, and went out to buy cloth.

Before 9:00 PM that night, Wang's Baby ran happily to my side. Sure enough, her mother's hands were fast, and Baby already had a black and white checkered scarf made of national goods lined flannel around her neck. Indeed, she was very proud and innocently showed it to me. I asked, "Baby! This scarf is made of Chinese goods, do you like it?" She said, "Yes, I heard my big sister say: Using national goods is patriotic!" Strange! A six-year-old girl also understands "national goods" and "patriotism." It can be seen that the psychology of most of our compatriots regarding the purchase and use of national goods has not been completely extinguished, but I have always been skeptical about Mrs. Wang's words.

National Goods Fashion Illustrated

— Ziwei

The cheongsam in this illustration is made of light green thin silk, a national product. The collar is cut into a square shape. The neckline, sleeve edges, and hem are all edged with dark green thin silk with the same pattern. This results in a novel, beautiful, and generous fashion. I hope ladies will try to make it.

A Lover's Gift

— Liu Zengwei

Zhang Yimin came out of his house excitedly, holding a large clothes box in his hand. The box had the words "XX National Goods Company" printed on it.

"She will definitely like it," he thought to himself, a smile constantly appearing on his face.

"Yimin, you should use national goods. Some national goods are also very good. Even if the goods are not so good, it is still happy for your conscience to use them." This was Xiuying—Yimin's lover's words, which he remembered again.

"Definitely, she will definitely like it," Yimin thought to himself again. After a while, he stopped in front of a house, raised one hand to the doorbell, and at the same time looked down at the thing in his other hand.

The door opened, and he quickly walked in.

"You're here. What did you bring?" A beautiful girl came out from inside. Seeing the box in his hand, she said this.

"Xiuying, guess," he said with a smile.

"Could it be your overcoat?"

"No."

"Is it your suit?"

"No, I listened to you and stopped wearing suits a long time ago."

"Then what is it?"

"It's for you."

"For me?"

"Yes, for you."

"Is it something imported again?"

"No, no. I know you don't like imported goods. How could I buy you imported goods again?" He said, and very proudly opened the box and took out a newly made garment.

"I bought you a new outfit." He took the garment and showed it to her, saying this.

"A new outfit that isn't imported?"

"No, I had this new outfit made from national goods at the China National Goods Company."

"Really?"

"Who's lying to you? If you don't believe me, look at the box that held the garment."

Xiuying indeed carefully examined the box. It had the words "China National Goods Company" printed on it, which made her believe that the new outfit was Chinese goods. She was extremely happy.

Short Story

The Day After the Fashion Show

— Qin Shouou

One winter, Shanghai held a grand Chrysanthemum Show. A fashion show was one of the important programs of the Chrysanthemum Show. Needless to say, the participants in the fashion show were of course the fashionable girls, and this time most of them were top students from the prestigious XX Girls' School.

The day after the fashion show, Mrs. Lin, the principal of XX Girls' School, suddenly summoned the dozen or so students who participated in the performance to her office.

"Ladies, you've worked hard. You've worked hard on another great work of national subjugation!" Principal Lin said with a bitter smile, saying something that seemed very comical.

The dozen or so girls were all stunned, vaguely pondering the novel term, "work of national subjugation."

"Weren't you all in the limelight yesterday? Liu Qianhong wore Parisian satin, Wang Feiyun wore some kind of American glitter yarn, Tao Jingfen wore Qiaoqi velvet, so beautiful, so extravagant. It's a pity you don't have high noses, green eyes, and golden red hair. Otherwise, you would have truly become Western beauties!"

Principal Lin's sharp teasing immediately made her top students realize their sins, and the dozen or so faces turned as red as if they had been painted with rouge.

"To be honest, you have misunderstood the term 'fashion'! Whether clothing is fashionable or not depends entirely on the change of style, not on the change of fabric. We Chinese produce quite a few silks and satins. The colors and patterns are not necessarily much worse than foreign goods. They can be used as fashionable fabrics. Although you are women, don't you know that using national goods is everyone's responsibility?" Speaking of this, Mrs. Lin's withered palms kept hitting the table. "Wake up! Stop being superstitious about Western goods. After the country is subjugated, you may think of your own sins!"

Mrs. Lin's words awakened the confused minds of these dozen or so beautiful girls. Everyone felt that "old lady" Lin's (the nickname of the principal) lesson today was truly a force that could not be disobeyed, and they all bowed and retreated willingly.

However, whether they can all use national goods depends on whether the environment can promote them!

Page 14

"I'll go try it on." She took the garment from Yimin's hand and ran inside.

After a while, she came out wearing the new outfit.

"How is it?" she said to Yimin with a smile.

"Very good! Very good!" Yimin said with a smile. "Didn't I tell you that national goods can also make very good new outfits? Do you believe it now?" Xiuying said to Yimin again.

"I believed it a long time ago, so I bought you this new outfit made of national goods," Yimin replied.

"Let's go inside and talk," Xiuying said, and went inside with Yimin.

Ramblings on Fashion

— Ke Ding'an

(Dedicated to women of the youth age)

The God of Era tells us: "The era progresses ceaselessly. If it stops, it will be the end of the world!" Then how should people of the youth age follow the era to be a new person in front of the era, instead of being a backward person behind the era?

Youth is valuable, which everyone admits. I think researching on clothing is also a great skill to keep youth. Then let's talk about the modernization of clothing.

In general, women of the youth age understand their time, and they are also very adept at meticulously crafting and manufacturing clothes; however, there is a shortcoming, which is that they specialize in using foreign fabrics, willing to be a promoter of foreign goods. Regarding this point, I would like to give advice to women of the youth age with my greatest respect. In the future, when you are making new clothes, it is better to choose national goods for the fabrics; because the current national silks and crepe have already surpassed the beauty of foreign goods, and they are unfolding a beautiful and bright appearance, waiting for you.

The time has shifted to summer, and of course the clothing also changes in style with the time. Let me introduce some fashions! It has become the current trend for women to like to wear long clothes, and shorts and long trousers have become equal opponents. I think that for the sake of preserving the dignity of women, shorts are very inappropriate under long clothes. If you wear shorts to stroll in the park, and you sit down on a park bench, the shorts will inevitably be pulled up, which seems very indecent. You may not feel it, but in the eyes of others, it looks like you are not wearing any trousers. My point is to lengthen the legs of the trousers. The diameter of the leg opening should not be more than seven inches. The length should be the same as the long clothes outside. The fabric should be the same color inside and out. It would be best to match the edges of the clothes and the legs of the trousers with symmetrical lace, which will add a lot of beauty.

Printed Georgette is a good fabric to embellish women. In summer, it is best to use a light green background with dark green flowers to make clothes. The shoulders should be made into a drooping cape, and the collar is not needed, but should be a bare-shoulder style. The waist should be thin, and the bottom should be made of pure black pleats, reaching the ankles. The high heels on the feet are best to be light green inlaid with dark green flowers.

A long dress made of pure black Georgette is very suitable for tall and fair women. There is no need to inlay or hem it. The cuffs should be attached to the arm bend with elastic bands. The part where the bands are attached should be enlarged, so that it can have a fluttering style in the evening breeze! The slits on both sides should be opened high, and the inside should be pleated. In this way, even if you run with large steps, you can't see the legs, and it doesn't hinder running and jumping. It is appropriate to wear black leather running shoes on your feet.

Using bright red fabrics in summer seems too fiery, but using them on girls around fifteen or sixteen years old can also reveal their true beauty. If you make a short-sleeved suit top with a bare neckline and chest, I think it would be absolutely wonderful!

Plaid double crepe is very suitable for women of the youth age. The making and color selection are all up to you. If you can use your brain, I can say, "You will definitely create a new atmosphere in the fashion of the sea!"

Fashion and Beautification

— Shi Dian

"Fashion" that fits the "times" is, in theory, naturally "perfect" and consistent with the principles of beautification. In reality, however, it's not entirely the case. Many so-called fashions are not necessarily beautifying, and some even fundamentally violate the principles of beautification.

The reason is simple: the general public is often blind. Women are no exception. When they see the novel clothing of so-called "fashionable people," they assume it must be the most beautifying fashion. Vanity often drives them to immediately imitate it. However, they are ignorant of whether it actually aligns with beautification and lack rational restraint.

True fashion, without a doubt, must conform to the principles of beautification and be designed and completed using scientific methods. We don't necessarily need silk fabrics or other expensive materials because they are not necessarily beautifying. Wearing them simply reveals a golden stench. Elegant and simple fabrics, combined with exquisite tailoring, draped on a slender, beautiful woman, with a graceful and ethereal quality, that is the democratic, fashionable, and artistic fashion!

National Goods Fashion Amidst National Crisis

— Ms. Hu Louzhen

The national crisis is becoming more pressing every day, and everyone should take responsibility for saving the country. This is absolutely undeniable. However, saving the country and loving the country cannot be achieved by empty words and grandstanding. The most important thing is to start with each of us!

The spring is bright, and its richness has reached its highest degree; in reality, it is already the "beginning of summer," so the weather has gradually moved from mild to warm and hot. At this moment, what exactly do we choose to make our national goods fashion? Here, we offer and introduce our summer fashion, roughly, for discussion with our female compatriots:

As we have said before, saving the country and loving the country should start with each individual. As this summer season begins, I think it is best to use "Freedom Cloth" or "Humiliation Cloth" for our national goods fabrics ("This is my subjective standard"), because these two are authentic national goods, their form is both beautiful and elegant, and their material is firm and solid. Based on my little experience in recent years, I think I am very satisfied. Regarding everything about it, I think it is by no means achievable with foreign goods!

At this time, when it is neither cold nor hot and the seasons are changing, wearing silk and satin may not be the right time, so Humiliation Cloth and Freedom Cloth still seem to be in their "prime." Its appreciation by people can last at least forty days. This can be said with certainty!

Fashion of Rural Women

— Guanshan

The sky is a dark blue, floating with some white clouds that drift along lightly. A breeze mixed with the fragrance of flowers blows on your face, and the sounds of birds fill the universe. Ah, what a spring evening, it is a time for a walk in the distance! If you have ever walked or strolled in the countryside, you will see that women over the age of thirty wear short shirts made of blue cloth, trousers made of white rough cloth, and on their heads are inferior scarves, with blue checks. Their feet are covered with shoes made of black twill, sitting there quietly doing their sewing. Women under the age of thirty wear red cloth pants, short shirts with striped cloth or cloth with flower heads, and most of their feet are bare, without a headscarf, but with a few yellow and white wildflowers inserted, happily and innocently handling their trivial housework, or playing with their children.

True patriots are rural women. They don't pay attention to beauty, they are very frugal. Red flowers and checks are considered the most beautiful to them. They don't need any silk or satin, but they can very naturally and mysteriously show their most beautiful fashion. They use national goods purely, but unlike urban women who shout about national goods but wear Indian silk on their bodies, I think urban women should take them as an example and follow their innocent and frugal fashion.

Fashion and National Goods

— Quan

The spring god has left, and the god of summer is gradually approaching, and the earth shows a harmonious and vigorous spirit.

Clumsy and heavy clothes, "time" will tell it, that it has fallen into disuse.

People must at this time remove the outdated clothes and put on light and floaty single-layer clothes.

At this moment, young girls will spare no money to choose the slender and moving fashion.

To make fashion is an important plan to adapt to the natural environment. Before you do it, don't forget one thing, that is, try to choose domestic materials as much as possible.

The motherland is already so fragile, and the compatriots of the three northeastern provinces and Rehe are already doing the real thing of being slaves to the country. We rely on heaven and earth (?) to still be able to breathe the air of freedom here, and we still have the opportunity to enjoy that "fashion", and we and the slaves of the country from the three northeastern provinces and Rehe are really as far apart as heaven and earth.

Living in the real paradise, we should quickly use domestic goods, otherwise, we are afraid that we will not suffer the same fate as these slaves of the country!

Moreover, good compatriots! Don't underestimate domestic goods. There are many beautiful and durable domestic goods, the prices are cheap, and they can save the country. When worn on the slender body of a girl, they show extra charm and gracefulness!

Young ladies! Why don't you pay attention to it!

My Family's National Goods Clothing

— Manbin

My family's national goods clothing is very interesting to talk about, so I might as well talk about it:

First, my husband's clothing has always been frugal, but the first thing he pays attention to is the quality of the material, so it is very difficult for me, who is his procurement officer. Sometimes, I casually buy some, but he doesn't trust them, and often doesn't allow them to be tailored. Once, after it was made, because he was afraid that it was not real national goods, he still didn't wear it. So later, I always went to his familiar manufacturers that he designated to buy the cloth, such as Sanyou and Hongxin, the silk and satin, such as Meiya, and the woolen fabrics, such as Zhanghua, so that he could rest assured. Second is the problem of tailoring. He is very particular about the times, but his times are just suitable, not long, not short, not wide, not narrow, so-called moderate. Once, he suddenly happily wore a student uniform made of national cloth and asked him why he learned the times. He said that it didn's matter what the times were, but it was just convenient.

Second, my own clothing also uses national goods as the only material, but I pay attention to the color and durability. The color should be elegant and never fade. Like our family, the budgeted clothing expenses total sixteen yuan per month, and it is not good to often add to them, so durability is the most important issue. I make my own clothes, so I don't care whether they are in fashion or not, but only whether they are comfortable or not.

Third, my youngest daughter, Quan'er, after participating in the clothing improvement meeting of the Family Renewing Society last time, developed the habit of loving to wear national goods clothing. What 212 or Snowflake tweed, are all the fabrics she loves to use. Recently, Mr. Xu Yangnan sent a newly-released cloth sample from Hongxin. Hongxin's colors contain three elements: elegance, simplicity, and tranquility. She was the first to try it. After trying it on, her colleagues at the bank all imitated her, and her classmates at Shanghai University of Commerce all imitated him. Later, Awei, Atong, A-Yuan, etc., all wanted to wear cloth clothes. Atong and A-Yuan especially love the serious attire of short clothes. When they wear short clothes and then put on leather shoes, they feel majestic and high-spirited. Also, I don't approve of children going shirtless, so Goose brand undershirts, not to mention adults can't do without them, every child in my family likes to wear them.

Autumn

Northeast Four Battalion Commanders

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Six: Coldly Observing the Sentimental Battlefield of Sweetness and Bitterness, Assessing the Two Sides, Secretly Agreeing on Three Years Amidst Treacherous Roads

As he spoke, he walked ahead. Guan and Yin followed closely behind. As they entered the main gate, Gui Zhi was just cleaning out the coal ash from the white stove, intending to dump it outside. When she saw Guan Yaowu, she stood there blankly, just staring. Guan Yaowu was also startled when he saw her and asked, "Aren't you Cousin Gui Zhi?" Gui Zhi replied, "Yes, are you Cousin Guan from the Guan family? I heard you were in Shanhaiguan, when did you return to Beiping? Oh my, Cousin Guan from the Guan family has come!" She put down the basket of coal ash and turned to run inside. Jiang Shi, asking about the Guan family cousin, came out to greet him. Guan Yaowu had already left Yin and Zhao and walked into the Yang family's courtyard. Seeing Jiang Shi, he called out, "Auntie!" Jiang Shi smiled and said, "Good heavens, it's Cousin Guan from the Guan family! How did you find us here?" Guan Yaowu walked into the house and first bowed deeply in greeting for the New Year. He saw that although the house was two humble rooms filled with old things, it was swept clean and tidy. He thought to himself, "No wonder Old Zhao keeps praising his neighbors, it's true, not just empty talk." Jiang Shi saw him looking around the house and smiled at him, "What do you think? Our family is getting poorer and poorer, and because of that, many relatives and friends don't visit anymore. How did you know we lived here, Cousin?" Guan Yaowu said, "We didn't know! It's just that Battalion Commander Zhao in the backyard is my colleague, and we are sworn brothers. We came here today to pay respects to Old Man Zhao for the New Year." Jiang Shi said, "This Battalion Commander Zhao here always talks about a Battalion Commander Guan. Who knew it was you, Cousin? What a coincidence! I moved here in the first half of last year, it's almost been a year." Guan Yaowu said, "I didn't know Auntie lived here, if I had known, I would have come to see you long ago." Saying that, he went to the backyard to pay his respects for the New Year. At this time, Yin Deren knew that the old girl was Battalion Commander Guan's cousin, and he deeply regretted making jokes in front of him. Even Zhao Ziqiang didn't dare to say another word. Guan Yaowu saw everything in his heart. After sitting in the backyard for a while, he came back to the front and chatted with Jiang Shi and her daughter. Jiang Shi was busy serving tea. They talked about family matters, and Guan Yaowu asked if his cousin had found a husband. (66)

Silk and Tea: Recent News of Spring Silkworms in Jiangsu and Zhejiang

(Yangzhong) Surrounded by rivers on all sides, in recent years, farmers have suffered losses in sericulture, and the silkworm capital has suffered heavy losses. They are very discouraged about sericulture. This year, the weather is abnormal, and the mulberry trees in the four villages have been slow to sprout. Now they are finally producing leaves. Those who have mulberry fields in the areas of Laolang Street, Matou Bridge, Sanmao Palace, Xinba, Xinglong Town, and Youfang Bridge have all borrowed capital to purchase improved varieties for breeding. The weather was sunny and warm when the ants were collected, and the silkworm ants developed well. The early batch has already had its third sleep and is producing leaves, while the late batch has just had its third sleep. It is a pity that the amount of feeding is limited.

(Xinchang) This year, the local silkworms that farmers bred early were completely abandoned due to damage from the weather, and the sericulture economy was in dire straits. Those who supplemented the late silkworms all cherished their capital to purchase breeds. Fortunately, the climate was sunny and warm, and the silkworm ants developed smoothly. The leaf production in the four villages was also abundant, and the leaf price was not high. Currently, the earliest silkworms in the Huangze area have entered a large sleep, the next earliest have had their third sleep and are producing leaves, and the latest have just started their third sleep and are waking up. Soon, the early silkworms will be able to make cocoons.

Gongbu Cocoon Shops Prepare to Open Weighing

The earliest cocoon season in Hangzhou is in the Linping, Gaosi, and Sanbao areas, where the early silkworms are about to form cocoons. Therefore, the cocoon shops in the Gongchen Bridge area are preparing to open weighing. However, only a few shops have rented out, reportedly only Weicheng and four or five others. They are currently renewing their cocoon certificates in preparation for weighing and collecting new cocoons.

Suian New Tea Continues to Open

Since the opening of Wenzhou green tea a few days ago, Suian Zhuangzhen Mei green tea continued to open yesterday. New goods from local Zhuang also opened new prices one after another. A total of more than 380 boxes of Zhen Mei and Zhen Mei needle tea were purchased by banks such as Xiehe and Tongfu. Suian Zhen Mei top plate opened at 155 yuan, local Zhuang Zhen Mei at 130 yuan, and needle tea at 45-6 yuan. Compared with the opening price last year, the main purpose is to change both into yuan. Most Chinese tea merchants have suffered losses. However, in recent days, the tea-producing areas of Suian, Huzhou, Xiaoshan, Dananshan, and Yang'ao have seen their hearts soften because the Shanghai market has failed to revitalize, and the market has plummeted by more than 10 yuan to 30 yuan.

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, there were more than 40 sources, and both retail and wholesale were still sluggish, resulting in few transactions as before. The market was flat. Su Tong geng and Nangang rice prices fell slightly. Although there were thin early rice deals, both the North and South Ocean gangs continued to handle them, but the number was not large. For example, the North Ocean gang only had 1,000 packages, and the South Ocean gang had 3-400 packages. Moreover, the methods adopted were different. The North Ocean selected high-quality materials, and the South Ocean agreed to the middle grade. The buying volume was still harsh, as if they would not take anything less than small. As a result, the prices of Qing, Yong, Songjiang, Sifeng, Xilian, and other goods fell by 2 cents. Only the prices of a small number of retail transactions seemed to be stable. Du Yangjian also fell slightly. The price of Yinbian Yuan lacked goods and had no honor or disgrace.

Flour Prices Fall Unanimously

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, all months showed signs of a unanimous decline. Because of the quotation for foreign wheat, both American and Kant fell by about 7-8 cents, the people's hearts were not uplifted after the opening. This month fell more than 1 cent, and the forward month fell by 1-1/2 cents. Until the later rounds, because large and small factories all sold, the amount was around 100,000 packages, and the market atmosphere was quiet again. Therefore, by the close, the forward month had fallen by 2 cents. By the afternoon opening, it was still flat and sluggish at first. Because transactions turned clear again, and the sellers were quiet, the hearts of outsiders turned stable again, returning nearly a cent from the morning's lowest price. According to the various factories, it was heard that they still had many chips in hand, so when they encountered an opportunity, they still could not avoid selling pressure. As a result, this month fell by 7 and a half cents, June fell by 1 cent and 2 and a half cents, July, August, and September fell by 1 cent, and October fell by 1 cent and 2 and a half cents.

New Wheat Has Hope for a Good Harvest

Yesterday, the wheat market was flat and sluggish. Because the quotation for foreign wheat fell by 7-8 cents, people's hearts in the market were unstable. However, current transactions ultimately had little development. Because the foreign wheat reserves of the various factories could still be used for two or three months, and domestic new wheat could also be harvested in another month, recent forecasts in the various producing areas have had good prospects for a good harvest. Therefore, the future of the wheat market is feared to be more difficult than the flour market. As a result, May and June did not open, July, August, and September each fell by 3 cents, and October did not open.

Qingzhong Bean Cakes Sell Smoothly

Because the bean cake market's factory cake quotations were higher than customer cakes, traders who distribute to the hinterland mainly used customer cakes. Moreover, customer cakes had better color and amount. Therefore, the buying side was also happy to accept them. Yesterday, only 2,000 pieces of Niuzhuang Xiyisheng cake were traded. Qingzhong cakes sold 10,000 pieces alone. Although the opening price was on the original pan, the atmosphere was quite stable.
